# Excalidraw Data

## Text Elements
You would have expected this behavior FAR away, where any linear distribution would 
seem like a thin line. But interestingly, due to the inverse square dependency and the symmetrical arguments
this happens as soon as you go outside the charge distribution.  ^VgI0Fhpv
